```markdown
## Magnesium for Period Pain: Complete Scientific Guide

### How Magnesium Works for Menstrual Cramps
- **Muscle Relaxation Mechanism**: Magnesium blocks calcium channels, preventing excessive uterine contractions
- **Nerve Function**: Modulates nerve transmission, reducing pain signal intensity
- **Anti-inflammatory Effects**: Reduces prostaglandin production and inflammatory responses

### Clinical Evidence
- Studies show 200-400mg daily magnesium reduces pain intensity by 45%
- Best absorption forms: Magnesium glycinate, citrate, malate
- Timing: Start 1 week before expected period

### Dosage & Safety Guidelines
| Form | Daily Dose | Best Time | Absorption Rate |
|------|------------|-----------|-----------------|
| Magnesium Glycinate | 200-400mg | Before bed | 90% |
| Magnesium Citrate | 300-500mg | With meals | 75% |
| Magnesium Oxide | 400-600mg | With meals | 30% |

### Food Sources & Meal Planning
**High Magnesium Foods (per 100g):**
- Dark chocolate: 228mg
- Pumpkin seeds: 262mg
- Spinach: 79mg
- Avocado: 58mg

**Sample Daily Menu for 400mg Magnesium:**
- Breakfast: Spinach omelet (80mg)
- Lunch: Quinoa salad with pumpkin seeds (120mg)
- Snack: Dark chocolate square (45mg)
- Dinner: Salmon with brown rice (155mg)
```

```html
function calculateRecommendation() {
    const painLevel = document.getElementById('painLevel').value;
    const symptoms = [];
    const checkboxes = ['nausea', 'headache', 'diarrhea', 'fatigue'];
    checkboxes.forEach(id => {
        if (document.getElementById(id).checked) symptoms.push(id);
    });

    const impact = document.querySelector('input[name="impact"]:checked')?.value || 'mild';

    let recommendation = generateRecommendation(painLevel, symptoms, impact);

    document.getElementById('recommendation').innerHTML = recommendation;
    document.getElementById('recommendation').style.display = 'block';

    // æ»šåŠ¨åˆ°ç»“æœ
    document.getElementById('recommendation').scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth' });
}

function generateRecommendation(painLevel, symptoms, impact) {

            â€¢ è½»åº¦è¿åŠ¨ï¼ˆæ•£æ­¥ï¼‰| Light exercise<br>
            â€¢ é•å‰‚ 200mgï¼ˆé¤åï¼‰| Magnesium 200mg with food
        `;
    } else if (painLevel <= 6) {
        urgency = 'ğŸŸ¡ ä¸­åº¦ç–¼ç—› | Moderate Pain';
        methods = `
            <strong>æ¨èæ–¹æ¡ˆï¼š</strong><br>
```

addEventListener('fetch', event => {
  event.respondWith(handleRequest(event.request))
})

async function handleRequest(request) {
  const url = new URL(request.url)

  // æ ‡é¢˜é‡å†™è§„åˆ™
  if (url.pathname.includes('natural-therapies')) {
    const response = await fetch(request)
    const rewriter = new HTMLRewriter()
      .on('title', { element: e => e.setInnerText('ç—›ç»ç–¼ç—›åŸç†çš„ç§‘å­¦è§£æ | Period Pain Mechanisms') })
      .on('h1', { element: e => e.setInnerText('ç—›ç»ç–¼ç—›åŸç†çš„ç§‘å­¦è§£æ') })
    return rewriter.transform(response)
  }

  // URLé‡å®šå‘è§„åˆ™
  if (url.pathname === '/en/natural-therapies') {
    return Response.redirect('https://www.periodhub.health/en/menstrual-pain-mechanisms', 301)
  }

  return fetch(request)
}

function calcDistance(userLat, userLng) {

```html
    const symptoms = [];
```

## ğŸ“Š Phase 3: æ•ˆæœç›‘æµ‹é…ç½®ï¼ˆå³æ’å³ç”¨ï¼‰

### A. Google Analytics 4 äº‹ä»¶è¿½è¸ª

#### åœ¨é¡µé¢å¤´éƒ¨æ·»åŠ ï¼š
```html
<!-- Google Analytics 4 - åŒ»ç–—å†…å®¹ä¸“ç”¨äº‹ä»¶ -->
<script async src="https://www.googletagmanager.com/gtag/js?id=GA_MEASUREMENT_ID"></script>
<script>
  window.dataLayer = window.dataLayer || [];
  function gtag(){dataLayer.push(arguments);}
  gtag('js', new Date());
  gtag('config', 'GA_MEASUREMENT_ID');

  // åŒ»ç–—å†…å®¹ä¸“ç”¨äº‹ä»¶è¿½è¸ª
  function trackMedicalEvent(eventName, contentType, painLevel = null) {
    gtag('event', eventName, {
      'event_category': 'Medical_Content',
      'event_label': contentType,
      'custom_parameter_1': painLevel,
      'page_title': document.title,
      'language': document.documentElement.lang || 'en'
    });
  }

  // è‡ªåŠ¨è¿½è¸ªå…³é”®äº¤äº’
  document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
    // ç´§æ€¥æŒ‡å—å±•å¼€
    const emergencyBox = document.querySelector('.emergency-relief-guide');
    if (emergencyBox) {
      emergencyBox.addEventListener('click', () => trackMedicalEvent('emergency_guide_used', 'pain_relief'));
    }

    // é•è¡¥å……å†…å®¹ç‚¹å‡»
    const magnesiumContent = document.querySelector('[data-content="magnesium"]');
    if (magnesiumContent) {
      magnesiumContent.addEventListener('click', () => trackMedicalEvent('magnesium_guide_viewed', 'supplement_info'));
    }

    // åŒ»ç–—å£°æ˜æŸ¥çœ‹
    const disclaimer = document.querySelector('.medical-disclaimer');
    if (disclaimer) {
      const observer = new IntersectionObserver((entries) => {
        entries.forEach(entry => {
          if (entry.isIntersecting) {
            trackMedicalEvent('medical_disclaimer_viewed', 'compliance');
          }
        });
      });
      observer.observe(disclaimer);
    }
  });
</script>
```
